Pkgs on Nix

Curated information about every package on Nix!

nixpkgs / plan9port - Plan 9 from User Space (aka plan9port) is a port of many Plan 9 programs from their native Plan 9 environment to Unix-like operating systems.

Homepage - https://9fans.github.io/plan9port/

License - MIT

Maintainers - Anderson Torres - Brandon Elam Barker - Emery Hemingway - Sigrid Solveig Haflínudóttir - Kovacsics Robert
